<p><span style="font-size:26px"><strong>Caucasians are Israelites According to Noah Webster of the Webster Encylopedia of Dictionaries (</strong><strong>©</strong> <strong>1958)</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">If you were a Caucasian, you are also an Israelite according to Noah Webster, and the Holy Bible. </span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">Webster Encyclopedia of Dictionaries (Copyright 1958 by the Literary Press, page 64), says “Caucasian” pertains to the white race originating from the Caucasus Mountains near the Black Sea.</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">The Holy Bible states that the House of Israel would be scattered north of the river Euphrates (1 Kings 14:15).  This promise was fulfilled when, in 721 B.C., all ten tribes were taken captive and driven by the Assyrians into the Caucasus Mountains located between the Caspian and Black Seas (2 Kings 17:6; 18:9-11).  Hosea 2:6 says,  “I will hedge up the way with thorns, and make a wall that she shall not find her paths.”  In this way God was making it clear that the tribes were not to return to Palestine.  As Israel left the mountains and migrated into Europe, and finally to North America, they became known as CAUCASIANS.  </span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px"></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“We must realize that our party’s most powerful weapon is racial tensions. By propounding into the consciousness of the dark races that for centuries they have been oppressed by whites, we can mold them to the program of the Communist Party. In America we will aim for subtle victory. While inflaming the Negro minority against the whites, we will endeavor to instill in the whites a guilt complex for their exploitation of the Negros. We will aid the Negroes to rise in prominence in every walk of life, in the professions and in the world of sports and entertainment. With this prestige, the Negro will be able to intermarry with the whites and begin a process which will deliver America to our cause.”</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px"><strong>Israel Cohen, A Racial Program for he Twentieth Century, 1912. Also in the Congressional Record, Vol. 103, p. 8559, June 7, 1957</strong></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px"><a href="/v3/r2/?url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuc3Rvcm1mcm9udC5vcmcvZm9ydW0vdDUyNzU2Lw==" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">https://www.stormfront.org/forum/t52756/</a></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px"><strong>Myron Fagan,</strong> a Jew substantiates the quote by Israel Cohen above. Here’s what he says about it:</span></span></p><p><div class="rotating_text_link" id="rotating_text_link_159"></div></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“Around 1910; one Israel Zengwill wrote a play entitled “The Melting- Pot.”</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“It was sheer propaganda to incite the Negroes and Jews because the play purportedly visualized how the American people were discriminating against, and persecuting Jews and Negroes.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“At that time nobody seemed to realize that it was a propaganda play.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“It was that cleverly-written.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“The propaganda was well wrapped-up in the truly great entertainment in the play and it was a big Broadway Hit.</span></span></p><p><div class="rotating_text_link" id="rotating_text_link_160"></div></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“Now in those years, the legendary Diamond Jim Brady used to throw a banquet at the famous Delmonico Restaurant in New York after the opening-performance of a popular play.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px"><strong>ILLUMINATI INFORMATION: DANGEROUS “ART” BEGINS TO EMERGE</strong></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“He threw such a party for the cast of “<strong>The Melting-Pot</strong>,” its author, producer, and chosen Broadway-celebrities. By then I’d already made a personal mark on the Broadway Theater and was invited to that party. There I met George Bernard Shaw and a Jewish writer named Israel Cohen.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“<strong>Zangwill, Shaw, and Cohen were the ones who created the Fabian Society</strong> in England and had worked closely with a <strong>Frankfurt Jew named Mordicai who had changed his name to Karl Marx</strong>; but remember, at that time both Marxism and Communism were just emerging and nobody paid much attention to either and nobody suspected the propaganda in the writings of those three really brilliant writers.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“At that banquet; Israel Cohen told me that he was then engaged in writing a book which was to be a <strong>follow-up on Zangwill’s “The Melting-Pot.”</strong></span></span></p><p><div class="rotating_text_link" id="rotating_text_link_161"></div></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“The title of his book was to be <strong>“A Racial-Program for the 20th Century.”</strong> At that time I was completely absorbed by my work as a playwright, and significant as that title was, its real objective never dawned on me nor was I interested in reading the book.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“But it suddenly hit me with the force of a hydrogen-bomb when I received a newspaper-clipping of an item published by the Washington D.C. Evening Star in May 1957. That item was a verbatim reprint of the following excerpt in Israel Cohen’s book “A Racial-Program for the 20th Century” and it read as I quote:</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px"><strong>ILLUMINATI INFORMATION: QUOTE FROM “A RACIAL PROGRAM…”</strong></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“We must realize that our party’s most powerful weapon is racial-tension.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“‘By propounding into the consciousness of the dark races, that for centuries they have been oppressed by the whites, we can move them to the program of the communist party.</span></span></p><p><div class="rotating_text_link" id="rotating_text_link_162"></div></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“In America; we will aim for subtle victory. While inflaming the Negro minority against the whites; we will instill in the whites a guilt-complex for their exploitation of the Negroes.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“We will aid the Negroes to rise to prominence in every walk of life, in the professions, and in the world of sports and entertainment. With this prestige; the Negro will be able to intermarry with the whites and begin a process which will deliver America to our cause.’</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px"><strong>ILLUMINATI INFORMATION: RECRUITING COMMUNISTS</strong></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“… Thus the authenticity of that passage in Cohen’s book was fully</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">established. But the one question that remained in my mind was whether it represented the official policy or plot of the Communist Party or just a personal expression of Cohen himself.</span></span></p><p><div class="rotating_text_link" id="rotating_text_link_163"></div></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“Hence I sought more proof and I found it in an official pamphlet published in 1935 by the New York Communist Party’s official Workers’ Library Publishers.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“That pamphlet was entitled: “The Negroes in a Soviet America.” It urged the Negroes to rise-up; form a soviet state in the south, and apply for admission to the Soviet Union. It contained a firm pledge that the revolt would be supported by all American “reds” and all so-called “liberals”.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px"><strong>“On page 38;</strong> it promised that a Soviet government would <strong>confer greater benefits to Negroes than to whites</strong> and again this official communist pamphlet pledged that; I quote: <strong>‘any act of discrimination or prejudice against a Negro will become a crime under the revolutionary law.’</strong></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“That statement proved that the excerpt in Israel Cohen’s book published in 1913 was an official-edict of the Communist Party and directly in line with the Illuminati-blueprint for world-revolution issued by Weishaupt and later by Albert Pike.</span></span></p>

<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">L. Rennap, Anti-Semitism and the Jewish Question (London, 1942), p. 31</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“Among his [Karl Marx’s] ancestors were Rabbis and Talmudists, men of learning and keen intellect.”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Henry Wickham Steed, in The American Hebrew (New York), December 9, 1927, p. 206</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“The peculiarly Jewish logic of his [Karl Marx’s] mind”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Henry Wickham Steed, in The American Hebrew (New York), December 9, 1927, p. 206</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“Mr. Wickham Steed lays the rise of Bolshevism at the doors of Jewry.”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">The Jewish Guardian (London), November 28, 1924, p. 4</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“The Bolshevik Revolution has emancipated the Jews as individuals”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Dr. Avrahm Yarmolinsky, in The Menorah Journal (New York), July 1928, p. 33</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“There are many Bolshevik leaders of Jewish extraction”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">D. L. Sandelsan, in The Jewish Chronicle (London), February 20, 1920, p. 22</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“There is no Jew who does not hope with all his heart that the Soviet Union will survive and be victorious”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Zionist Review (London: Zionist Federation of Great Britain and Ireland), September 26, 1941, p. 7</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“Communism and internationalism are in truth and in fact great virtues. Judaism may be justly proud of these virtues”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Harry Watan, A Program for the Jews and an Answer to All Anti-Semites (New York: Committee for the Preservation of the Jews, 1939), p. 80</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“If the tide of history does not turn toward Communist internationalism … then the Jewish race is doomed.”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">George Marlen, Stalin, Trotsky, or Lenin (New York, 1937), p. 414</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“The [Jewish] Commissaries were formerly political exiles. They had been dreaming of revolution for years in their exile in Paris, in London, in New York, in Berlin, everywhere and anywhere. They saw in the Bolshevist Movement an opportunity of realizing the extreme ideas of Communism and internationalism to which their fate had compelled them.”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Dr. D. S. Pazmanik, in The Jewish Chronicle (London), September 5, 1919, p. 14</span></span></p>

<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Jewish Voice (New York: National Council of Jewish Communists), January 1942, p. 16</span></span></p>

<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">The Congress Bulletin, (New York: American Jewish Congress), January 5, 1940, p. 2</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“There is no official anti-Semitism in Russia; anti-Semitism in Russia is a crime against the State.”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Dr. Chalm Weizmann, The Jewish People and Palestine (London: Zionist Organization, 1939), p. 7</span></span></p>

<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Harry Sacher, in The Jewish Review (London), June-August 1932, p. 43</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">“The Jews have a right to subordinate to themselves the rest of mankind and to be the masters over the whole earth. This is the historic destiny of the Jews”</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Harry Waton, A Program for the Jews and an Answer to All Anti-Semites (New York Committee for the Preservation of the Jews, 1939), pp. 99-100</span></span></p>

<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">Leon Dennen, in The Menorah Journal (New York, July-September 1932, p. 105</span></span></p>

<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">BENJAMIN FRANKLIN</span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><a href="/v3/r2/?url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuYml0Y2h1dGUuY29tL3ZpZGVvL3hxMlR2ZXd4aHd6Ui8=" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">https://www.bitchute.com/video/xq2TvewxhwzR/</a></span></span></p>
<p><strong><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">Sarah, The Wife Of Abraham, Had Pure White Skin</span></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><a href="/v3/r2/?url=aHR0cDovL2V1cm9mb2xrcmFkaW8uY29tLzIwMTgvMDIvMTQvZGVhZC1zZWEtc2Nyb2xscy1hbmFseXNpcy1jZW5zb3JlZC16b2cv" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://eurofolkradio.com/2018/02/14/dead-sea-scrolls-analysis-censored-zog/</a></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:22px">The Essenes were law-keepers, unlike the Pharisees and Sadducees.  (Note that the Essenes were NOT a Jewish sect.   Josephus tells us that the Essenes were composed of pure-blooded Judahites.  In essence, they were the first monastic sect of Christianity.)</span></span></p><p><div class="rotating_text_link" id="rotating_text_link_209"></div></p>
<p><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">The real reason the Essenes left Jerusalem is because they were being persecuted by the Pharisees and Sadducees.   The REAL REASON for the Dead Sea Scrolls cover-up is because they reveal that the Israelites were Caucasians.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">“<em>In the seventh Dead Sea scroll, whoever wrote this extolled Sarah’s perfections from head to foot and while it was written in prose poem, the description as it appeared in the news media was as follows:</em></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><em>    `<strong>Her skin was pure white;</strong></em></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><em>     She had long and lovely hair;</em></span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><em>     Her limbs were smooth and rounded and</em></span></span></p><p><div class="rotating_text_link" id="rotating_text_link_210"></div></p>
